< review>
This review is directed toward Nick Alexander and the staff at N.A. Mini.

This is an updated and edited version of a earlier review.
Upfront I apologize for the length and the complexity of this piece, I want to provide an accurate account of my experience and personal opinions for all to understand my position.

I set up an appointment to get my car serviced for an engine oil change at 10:00 a.m. on Tuesday 23rd 2018.

This was my experience:

- Arrived at 10:00 a.m., checked in, got briefed on the service by Eli (my representative). I was told that the service would take "2 - 3 hours", and the price tag would be $380, because an up-charge for new spark plugs was recommended. I agreed to the terms and service (sigh). Later, I find out I didn't need the spark plugs for another 7 - 8 thousand miles, based  on standard recommendation.

- 12:58 P.M., waiting by the lounge and expecting things to be finishing up. I send my rep a text, no response. Wait another 45 minutes, wrote this review because I didn't have any idea what was going on with my car.

- 2:00 P.M. I walk up to the service counter to meet with my rep, and I wait because he's with another customer. In between, a service manager (Lori, I believe) approaches me and tries to diagnose why I wrote a less than favorable review on Yelp. I explained it was due to a few factors, which I've listed below.

- 2:15 P.M. after my prolonged discussion with Lori, my rep then asks me to go and check out the car because there's a problem with the vehicle. My rep and the mechanic on duty explain that coolant is leaking from its container down my engine. They at this point suggest that I change the hose, and that the quote for this service will cost an additional $300. I didn't agree to any more service.

- 2:25 P.M., my rep said he'll finish up the car, just needs to be washed and then I'll be good to go. 3:00 P.M., I'm finally reached by my rep in person to let me know my car is ready for payment and pick up. I left the dealership around 3:06 P.M. (5 hrs to change engine oil and spark plugs).

Facts:
- I waited 5 hrs for completion of the services requested
- I received no communication or updates about my car via
text or phone
- Spark plugs were never checked to see if they needed
replacement prior to agreement of change service
- I paid an additional $300 for parts and service I didn't
need, instead of paying for the coolant hose that should
have been priority.
- I was told about a serious problem on my car after more
than 4 hrs of waiting
- I wrote this review as a result of all the above mentioned

Expectations for service:
- Honesty, integrity
- Communications and updates (frequent and informative)
- Good customer service, timely handling of service;
I expected service to be completed within the time range
I was given (If I was told 4 - 5 hrs, I would have complied)
- Equal value in exchange for payment
- Positive value and experience for my service visit

Reality of service:
- Ambiguity, vagueness
- Infrequent communication and/or updates on my car's
status, late communication on required service
- Friendly customer service and staff. Bad time management
and sensitivity to timely completion of service
- Costly price in exchange for services
- Mid-range (below average) value, lack luster experience
for my service visit

The Future:

I still need to change my coolant hose, but am really weary about returning to the dealership for service. I don't want to dedicate additional time to have another prolonged visit, nor am I willing to pay ($300) an exorbitant price on fixing my car to stop a leak. I'm not sure if my car is nominally functional, and am concerned to drive it until I can fix the issue that was brought to my attention so late. I'm considering other dealerships and service centers to help me out with my current situation.

Thanks All.<//review>

David Inturralde.  Ask for that name.  You will get someone who will treat you with respect and patience.  No hard sell.  You are always comfortable with David.  He will get you the car YOU want.  He will hunt down the best terms for your situation.  He stays on top of it all, and when he says he will call you, he calls you.  (Novelty in this town.)  He will also do his very best to get your car to you as quickly as possible so you can start having fun with it.

I picked Alexander Mini on two points:  a friend has a relative working there and the reviews for this dealership beat the others around it.  The reviews were not wrong.  Through out, by every person, I have been treated well.  There has never been an uncomfortable moment.  I never felt someone was out for a buck.  This is Mini, it sells itself.  The people involved just slide you into the one that you want.

I can already say something about the service department:  My car was on the boat and on its way when I test drove a Mini on a Saturday (David did a search of cars available and found it for me).  The car didn't arrive at the dealership until the following Friday.  Knowing a buyer was excited to get their car, the service department had that car prepped, hood stripes on and ready to roll shortly after I got there, a little after 9:00 the next day.  These guys are quick.

Even though I have a Mini dealership closer to home, I'll be coming back here for my service.

Thank you everyone and especially thank you David.  I had a great experience and had a great first day with my Mini.

UPDATE!

First let me put in a disclaimer:  Things happen.   Sometimes things are not perfect.

That out of the way we can talk about what happened when my new Mini's engine was found to be defective.

My check engine light came on after about 2500 miles.  I stayed on top of it and go the car in.  Check engine lights are there for a reason and you will soon read why.

The service department found misfires but couldn't find the reason.  Ok, chalk that one up to a "phantom" code showing.  I go my merry way.

Check engine light comes on again.  This time my service advisor, Ron, said he wanted to really see what was going on.  I was handed a Mini Clubman and sent home.

The service department found my engine was defective and Ron put in a request to get it replaced.  At first everything looked like it would go smoothly.  Ron kept me informed every few days.

The problem was with Mini Corporate.  They were a very slow with communicating with Nick Alexander, and we ended up with no idea when I would get an engine.  I hit Mini USA's Facebook page and Mini USA got a hold of me next day.  Bill at Mini USA launched an investigation and the engine was at the dealership the very next week.
(Slowness at the dealership is not always the dealership's fault, but the corporate entity they depend on, and corporate is dependent on their vendors.)

The mechanics at NIck Alexander worked some magic once that engine was in their hands.  The engine was at the dealership noon Monday and I was called noon Wednesday that my car was ready.

The aftercare at this dealership is great.  They communicate with you and try hard to make whatever repairs or service as little an inconvenience as possible.  I overheard (sorry for that) their interactions with other people and this crew goes out of their way to help.

Thank you to Ron and the service crew.  Next time I see you it will be for scheduled service....I promise.< /review>

< text>
2/5/20 Please read the update below, too. üòä
This is a high quality place. They have a reflecting room stocked with cold water with orange slices in it, as well as tea bags for hot tea and a nice sitting area with magazines so you can unwind a little before your massage. The receptionists are always polite, helpful, and if you go regularly like me, they do their best to greet you by name. The restrooms are nicely decorated with shelves so you have a place to put your purse. They are always clean and are actually larger than most homes restrooms.  The massage room is nice, not as well decorated, but I am not there for the pictures anyway.  There are hooks and a large square seat for your clothes and personal items. The table is heated and the height is adjustable, with dimmers on the lights. They are careful to be sensitive to any allergies that you may have. My therapist is excellent. He actually researches on his own time stretches and exercises to help me improve my flexibility.  He is very professional and my chiropractor loves him! üôÇ
UPDATE:  At the risk of him getting too busy to fit me in, I have to say Patrick, my massage therapist, is the best! All of the things I said above are about him. And not only does he stay studied up, he also gives healthy diet and herb tips, and encourages me to keep up on my water intake.  He always reminds me that he isn't a doctor, but I trust him, because I know he is serious about his career. He is very professional. He lets you know what he is doing, helps you realize when you aren't relaxed and helps you learn how to, and if you want to talk, he will engage you. If you don't want to talk, he respects that, too. < review>
I've been getting oil changes here for a few years usually with an appointment. I've always got great service so when I noticed I was leaking fluid and the transmission was acting funny, I took it to Meineke's. They diagnosed the problem and replaced a leaking transmission line. It was a labor intensive job which took over a day to repair.  Frank, the employee I interfaced with, did an excellent job of working with the warranty company and getting me a car rental (included in warranty). So far I have not noticed any problems with the transmission. If I do, Frank told me to bring it back and they will repair whatever is necessary and include it in the same warranty job so I wouldn't have to pay the deductible again. I would recommend them as a repair shop.

As a follow on, I did return the car because the transmission was not shifting well. They diagnosed and fixed the problem at no cost. Great job!< /review>

I went to Meineke in Ventura (4519 telephone rd) for a standard oil change on 4/29/2014 with 178,026 miles. After driving my vehicle for a couple of months (10/16/2014 with 182,826 miles on odometer: 4 800 miles since my last oil change) I noticed my car lossing power. Immediately, I begin to try to get off the freeway to address the issue but my engine began to knock, shut down and I threw it into neutral and coasted off the freeway. I was able to get a mechanic to look at it and was informed that I did not have an oil filter.
